</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Walgreens Boots Alliance Reports Fiscal 2025 First Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Delivering Progress on Strategic Priorities; Maintaining Full Year Adjusted EPS Guidance </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>First quarter financial results </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">First quarter loss per share<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> was $0.31 versus loss per
share of $0.08 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Loss per share in the current quarter includes costs related to the Footprint Optimization Program and an <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> charge for
fair value adjustments on variable prepaid forward derivatives related to the monetization of Cencora shares </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

earnings per share of $0.66 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter driven by lower U.S. retail sales and prior year sale-leaseback gains, partly offset by cost savings and growth in U.S. Healthcare </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">First quarter sales increased 7.5&nbsp;percent year-over-year to $39.5&nbsp;billion, up 6.9&nbsp;percent on a
constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Fiscal 2025 guidance* </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Maintaining fiscal 2025 adjusted EPS<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> guidance of $1.40 to
$1.80, with growth in U.S. Healthcare and International more than offset by a decline in U.S. Retail Pharmacy, a higher adjusted effective tax rate, and lower contributions from sale-leaseback and Cencora earnings </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">DEERFIELD, Ill. &#151; January&nbsp;10, 2025 &#151; Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA) today announced financial results for the first quarter of
fiscal 2025, which ended November&nbsp;30, 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Chief Executive Officer Tim Wentworth said: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our first quarter results reflect our disciplined execution against our 2025 priorities: stabilizing the retail pharmacy by optimizing our footprint,
controlling operating costs, improving cash flow and continuing to address reimbursement models.&#148; said Tim Wentworth, Chief Executive Officer, Walgreens Boots Alliance. &#147;While our turnaround will take time, our early progress reinforces
our belief in a sustainable, retail <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pharmacy-led</FONT> operating model.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of First Quarter Results
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA first quarter sales increased 7.5&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $39.5&nbsp;billion, an
increase of 6.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting sales growth across all business segments. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:26%">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">*</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company does not provide a reconciliation for non-GAAP estimates on a forward-looking basis where it is
unable to provide a meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort and the Company is unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">&#147;Adjusted,&#148; &#147;constant currency&#148; and free cash flow amounts are non-GAAP financial measures. See the
appendix to this release for a discussion of non-GAAP financial measures, including a reconciliation to the most closely correlated GAAP measure </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First quarter operating loss was $245&nbsp;million compared to an operating loss of $39&nbsp;million in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted operating income<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> was $593&nbsp;million compared to adjusted operating income of $687&nbsp;million in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. The increase in operating loss reflects higher costs related to the Footprint Optimization Program in the U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment, and both operating loss and adjusted operating income<SUP
STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> reflect lower U.S. retail sales and lapping prior year sale-leaseback gains, partly offset by cost savings initiatives and growth in the U.S. Healthcare segment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net loss in the first quarter was $265&nbsp;million compared to a net loss of $67&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter, primarily driven by higher operating loss. Adjusted net earnings<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> decreased 23.0&nbsp;percent to $440&nbsp;million, down 23.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting lower
adjusted operating income. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Loss per share in the first quarter was $0.31 compared to loss per share of $0.08 in the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted EPS<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> was $0.51 compared to adjusted EPS<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2 </SUP>of $0.66 in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter reflecting a decrease of 23.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash used for operating
activities was $140&nbsp;million in the first quarter, a $141&nbsp;million improvement compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Operating cash flow was negatively impacted by seasonal inventory build in the U.S.,
UK and Germany, and legal payments of $137&nbsp;million. Free cash flow<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> was negative $424&nbsp;million, a $363&nbsp;million improvement compared with the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter primarily driven by a decrease in capital expenditures of $223&nbsp;million and higher adjusted operating income excluding sale-leaseback, which does not impact free cash flow. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business Segments </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>U.S. Retail Pharmacy </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="76%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt" ALIGN="center">

<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>

<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">$</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="right">28,944</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted operating income <SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">$</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="right">441</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">$</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="right">694</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment had first quarter sales of $30.9&nbsp;billion, an increase of 6.6&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Comparable sales increased 8.5&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pharmacy sales increased 10.4&nbsp;percent and comparable pharmacy sales increased 12.7&nbsp;percent in the quarter, each benefiting from higher branded drug
inflation and prescription volume. Comparable prescriptions filled in the first quarter increased 2.3&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter while comparable prescriptions excluding immunizations increased
3.5&nbsp;percent. Total prescriptions filled in the quarter, including immunizations, adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents increased 1.5&nbsp;percent to 316.3&nbsp;million. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Retail sales decreased 6.2&nbsp;percent and comparable retail sales decreased 4.6&nbsp;percent compared with the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting a weaker cough cold flu season and lower sales in discretionary categories. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted
operating income decreased 36.4&nbsp;percent to $441&nbsp;million compared to $694&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, driven primarily by lower retail sales and lapping prior year sale-leaseback gains,
partially offset by cost savings. </P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The International segment had first quarter sales of $6.4&nbsp;billion, an increase of 10.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including a favorable currency impact of 3.6&nbsp;percent. Sales increased 6.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, with the Germany wholesale business growing 11.3&nbsp;percent and Boots UK
sales growing 4.5&nbsp;percent. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Boots UK comparable pharmacy sales increased 10.9&nbsp;percent compared with the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Boots UK comparable retail sales increased 8.1&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter with growth across all categories. Boots.com sales grew
30&nbsp;percent, or 23&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, aided by strong Black Friday performance and representing 22&nbsp;percent of Boots total retail sales. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted operating income increased 17.9&nbsp;percent to $168&nbsp;million, an increase of 16.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, led by strong retail performance in Boots UK and growth in Germany, partly offset by cost inflation and technology investments. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating loss was $325&nbsp;million compared to $436&nbsp;million in the prior year period reflecting improved performance at VillageMD and Shields. Adjusted

quarter. Adjusted EBITDA of $70&nbsp;million improved by $109&nbsp;million versus the prior year quarter reflecting higher contribution from VillageMD risk-based and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">fee-for-service</FONT></FONT> business and growth at Shields. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Conference Call

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">ENDS </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Notes to Editors:
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Walgreens Boots
Alliance (Nasdaq: WBA) is an integrated healthcare, pharmacy and retail leader serving millions of customers and patients every day, with a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">175-year</FONT> heritage of caring for communities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A trusted, global innovator in retail pharmacy with approximately 12,500 locations across the U.S., Europe and Latin America, WBA plays a critical role in the
healthcare ecosystem. Through dispensing medicines, improving access to pharmacy and health services, providing high quality health and beauty products and offering anytime, anywhere convenience across its digital platforms, WBA is shaping the
future of healthcare in the thousands of communities it serves and beyond. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA employs approximately 312,000 people, with a presence in eight countries
and consumer brands including: Walgreens, Boots, Duane Reade, No7 Beauty Company and Benavides. The Company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. In fiscal 2024,
WBA scored 100% on the Disability Equality Index for disability inclusion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">More Company information is available at www.walgreensbootsalliance.com. </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following information provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under
the SEC rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (GAAP). The Company has provided the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which are not calculated or presented in accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and
presented in accordance with GAAP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because
management has evaluated the Company&#146;s financial results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency translation, as applicable, and believes that the supplemental
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the Company from period to period and trends in the Company&#146;s historical
operating results. The Company also uses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures as a basis for certain compensation programs it sponsors. These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial
measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press release. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates to the most directly comparable GAAP financial
measures on a forward-looking basis where it is unable to provide a meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of
forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet occurred, are out of the Company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, such as unusual <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> charges, tax expenses, and
material litigation expenses, and that would impact diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the Company is unable to address the probable significance of the
unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially from the corresponding GAAP financial measures.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Constant currency </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company also presents certain
information related to current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating current period results at the
foreign currency exchange rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The Company presents such constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the U.S. reporting in currencies other than the U.S.
dollar and such presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">10 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Comparable sales </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the Company&#146;s U.S. Retail Pharmacy and International segments, comparable sales are defined as sales from stores that have been open for at least
twelve consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days, including due to looting or store damage, and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster, in the past twelve months as well as <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. Comparable sales in constant currency exclude wholesale sales in Germany and sales from dispositions. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">E-commerce</FONT> sales include digitally initiated sales
online or through mobile applications. Relocated stores are not included as comparable sales for the first twelve months after the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable sales for the first twelve months after acquisition or
conversion, when applicable, whichever is later. Comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales, comparable retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions and comparable number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent
prescriptions refer to total sales, pharmacy sales, retail sales, number of prescriptions and number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, respectively. The method of calculating comparable sales varies across
the retail industry and our method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same as other retailers&#146; methods. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With respect to the
International segment, comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail sales, are presented on a constant currency basis, which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Refer to the discussion above
in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant currency calculations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Key Performance Indicators </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company considers certain metrics, such as comparable sales (in constant currency), comparable pharmacy sales (in constant currency), comparable retail
sales (in constant currency), comparable number of prescriptions, comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, and comparable prescriptions excluding immunizations to be key performance indicators because the
Company&#146;s management has evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance indicators presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the
Company from period to period and trends in its historical operating results. These key performance indicators should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP
financial measures presented herein. These measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled performance indicators used by other companies. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Amounts may
not add due to rounding. All percentages and ratios have been calculated using unrounded amounts. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Footprint Optimization charges are costs associated with a formal restructuring plan. These charges are
primarily recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring activity.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets and stock-based
compensation fair valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangible assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks, developed technology and contract intangibles.
Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The revenue generated by the associated
intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular period unless an intangible asset
becomes impaired, or the estimated useful life of an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. The stock-based
compensation fair valuation adjustment reflects the difference between the fair value based remeasurement of awards under purchase accounting and the grant date fair valuation. Post-acquisition compensation expense recognized in excess of the
original grant date fair value of acquiree awards are excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as these arise from acquisition-related accounting requirements or agreements, and are not reflective of normal
operating activities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition and disposition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger,
acquisition and divestitures related activities recorded in Operating loss within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. Examples of such costs include deal costs, severance, stock-based compensation, employee transaction success
bonuses, and other integration related exit and disposal charges. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. These costs are significantly
impacted by the timing and complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. As part of the amendment to the VillageMD Secured Loan executed in
the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2024, Walgreen Co. and VillageMD agreed to terminate certain intercompany leases resulting in an early termination charge of $107&nbsp;million incurred by VillageMD within the U.S. Healthcare segment and a
corresponding gain recognized within the U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment. The impacts of the intercompany lease termination eliminate in consolidation. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to equity earnings (loss) in Cencora consist of the Company&#146;s proportionate share of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments reported by Cencora consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Adjustments are recorded to Equity earnings (loss) in Cencora within the
Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">5</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Certain legal and regulatory accruals and settlements relate to significant charges associated with certain
legal proceedings, including legal defense costs. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation
of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">6</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company&#146;s U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment inventory is accounted for using the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">last-in-first-out</FONT></FONT></FONT> (&#147;LIFO&#148;) method. This adjustment represents the impact on Cost of sales as if the U.S. Retail Pharmacy
segment inventory is accounted for using <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-in</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-out</FONT> (&#147;FIFO&#148;) method. The LIFO provision is affected by changes in inventory quantities, product mix,
and manufacturer pricing practices, which may be impacted by market and other external influences. Therefore, the Company cannot control the amounts recognized or timing of these items. These charges are recorded within Cost of sales within the
Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">7</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>

charges are primarily recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring
activity. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2024 and were $162&nbsp;million in the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2023. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

Condensed Statements of Earnings. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because these do not relate to the ordinary course of the Company&#146;s business. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

in the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because these do not relate to the ordinary course of the Company&#146;s business. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

investments consist of the proportionate share of certain equity method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the Company&#146;s
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments. These charges are recorded in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Post-tax</FONT> earnings (loss) from other equity method investments within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of
Earnings. Although the Company may have shareholder rights and board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating to equity method investments are not intended to imply that the
Company has direct control over their operations and resulting revenue and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations in that they do not reflect all revenue and expenses of these
equity method investees. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

VillageMD Secured Loan that consolidated certain VillageMD obligations to the Company, modified certain interest and fee terms, and provided VillageMD with additional borrowing capacity. These intercompany credit facilities eliminate in
consolidation. The Company applies the legal claim approach to the attribution of intercompany transactions to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-controlling</FONT> interests. The amendment of the VillageMD Secured Loan increased the
Company&#146;s claim on VillageMD&#146;s net assets resulting in a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-controlling</FONT> interest benefit. The amendment and related
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> benefit to the Company are not indicative of normal operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company reconciles Adjusted EBITDA for the U.S. Healthcare segment to Operating loss as the closest GAAP
measure for the segment profitability. The Company does not measure Net earnings attributable to Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. for its segments. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition and disposition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger,
acquisition and divestitures related activities recorded in Operating loss within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. Examples of such costs include deal costs, severance, stock-based compensation, employee transaction success
bonuses, and other integration related exit and disposal charges. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. These costs are significantly
impacted by the timing and complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. As part of the amendment to the VillageMD Secured Loan executed in
the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2024, Walgreen Co. and VillageMD agreed to terminate certain intercompany leases resulting in an early termination charge of $107&nbsp;million incurred by VillageMD within the U.S. Healthcare segment and a
corresponding gain recognized within the U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment. The impacts of the intercompany lease termination eliminate in consolidation. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets and stock-based
compensation fair valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangible assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks, developed technology and contract intangibles.
Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The revenue generated by the associated
intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular period unless an intangible asset
becomes impaired, or the estimated useful life of an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. The stock-based
compensation fair valuation adjustment reflects the difference between the fair value based remeasurement of awards under purchase accounting and the grant date fair valuation. Post-acquisition compensation expense recognized in excess of the
original grant date fair value of acquiree awards are excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as these arise from acquisition-related accounting requirements or agreements, and are not reflective of normal
operating activities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Certain legal and regulatory accruals and settlements relate to significant charges associated with certain
legal proceedings, including legal defense costs. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation
of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">5</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Footprint Optimization charges are costs associated with a formal restructuring plan. These charges are
primarily recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring activity.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">6</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Transformational Cost Management Program charges are costs associated with a formal restructuring plan. These
charges are primarily recorded in Selling, general and administrative expenses within the Consolidated Condensed Statements of Earnings. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring
activity. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">7</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Includes GAAP stock-based compensation expense excluding expenses related to acquisition-related amortization
and acquisition-related costs. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>EQUITY EARNINGS (LOSS) IN CENCORA </U></B></P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="76%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property,
plant and equipment (capital expenditures), plus acquisition related payments and incremental pension payments made in that period. This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not
deduct the payments required for debt service and other contractual obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to the
Consolidated Condensed Statement of Cash Flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">#&#8195;#&#8195;#&#8195;#&#8195;# </P>
